    <div class="container-up-xl">
     <div class="row justify-content-center">
      <div class="col col-md-auto">
       <h3>
        What is Flippa?
       </h3>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="row">
      <div class="col-md-4 mt-5">
       <img alt="Icon global" src="https://d1zazrti94enmy.cloudfront.net/assets/homepage/icon-global-e99f708a62fc9620c4601b4352d649e152c388b88ef37c414f175174bc0754d0.svg"/>
       <h5 class="my-4">
        A community of owners, investors, creators and makers
       </h5>
       <p>
        Flippa is a global online marketplace where individuals and business owners buy and sell websites, online businesses and other digital real estate.
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="col-md-4 mt-5">
       <img alt="Icon exchange" src="https://d1zazrti94enmy.cloudfront.net/assets/homepage/icon-exchange-c7227ffbf43e631e874ed7bceabffde5d18be6338dc3bd9d34b91d8df95ca4ab.svg"/>
       <h5 class="my-4">
        A peer-to-peer platform
       </h5>
       <p>
        On Flippa, sellers are selling their passion projects, side hustles and online businesses. We make the process super easy by connecting you with these sellers and streamlining the negotiation and transaction.
       </p>

       <h5 class="my-4">
